logger = logging.getLogger(__name__)


def escape_md(text: str) -> str:
    """Escapes special characters for MarkdownV2."""
    special_chars = r"\_*[]()~`>#+-=|{}.!"
    return "".join(f"\\{c}" if c in special_chars else c for c in str(text))


def get_profile_keyboard(user_id: int, notifs_on: bool = True):
    notif_label = "рџ”” РЎРїРѕРІС–С‰РµРЅРЅСЏ: РІРєР»" if notifs_on else "рџ”• РЎРїРѕРІС–С‰РµРЅРЅСЏ: РІРёРєР»"
    keyboard = [
        [InlineKeyboardButton(text="в• РџС–РґС‚СЂРёРјР°С‚Рё РќРµС‚РёРєР°", callback_data="menu_donate")],
        [
            InlineKeyboardButton(text=notif_label, callback_data="profile_notifications"),
            InlineKeyboardButton(text="рџ‘Ґ Р РµС„РµСЂР°Р»", callback_data="profile_referral")
        ],
        [InlineKeyboardButton(text="в¬…пёЏ РњРµРЅСЋ", callback_data="back_to_menu")]
    ]
    return InlineKeyboardMarkup(inline_keyboard=keyboard)


@router.callback_query(F.data == "menu_profile")
@router.message(Command("profile"))
async def show_profile(event: Union[types.Message, types.CallbackQuery]):
    user_id = event.from_user.id
    user_data = await db.get_user(user_id)
    if not user_data:
        # If user_data is not found, we can't proceed.
        # For a message event, we might want to inform the user or log.
        # For a callback, we might answer the callback.
        if isinstance(event, types.CallbackQuery):
            await event.answer("РџРѕРјРёР»РєР°: РґР°РЅС– РєРѕСЂРёСЃС‚СѓРІР°С‡Р° РЅРµ Р·РЅР°Р№РґРµРЅРѕ.", show_alert=True)
        else:
            await event.answer("РџРѕРјРёР»РєР°: РЅРµ РІРґР°Р»РѕСЃСЏ Р·Р°РІР°РЅС‚Р°Р¶РёС‚Рё РІР°С€ РїСЂРѕС„С–Р»СЊ.")
        return

    stats = await db.get_user_stats(user_id)
    has_premium = await is_premium(user_id, event.bot)

    reg_date = user_data.get("created_at", "РќРµРІС–РґРѕРјРѕ")
    if reg_date != "РќРµРІС–РґРѕРјРѕ":
        try:
            dt = datetime.fromisoformat(reg_date)
            reg_date = dt.strftime("%d.%m.%Y")
        except Exception:
            pass

    safe_name = html.escape(user_data.get("full_name") or "РќРµРІС–РґРѕРјРѕ")
    safe_username = html.escape(user_data.get("username") or "Р±РµР· СЋР·РµСЂРЅРµР№РјСѓ")
    safe_reg_date = html.escape(reg_date)
    safe_watched = stats["watched_count"]
    safe_watchlist = stats["watchlist_count"]
    safe_ratings = stats["ratings_count"]
    safe_avg_rating = stats["avg_rating"]
    safe_top_position = stats["top_position"]
    safe_points = user_data.get("points", 0)

    expert_eye = "рџ‘ЃвЂЌрџ—Ё <b>Expert Eye</b> " if await db.has_achievement(user_id, "expert_eye") else ""
    community_voice = "рџ“ў <b>Community Voice</b> " if await db.has_achievement(user_id, "community_voice") else ""
    achievements_text = f"\nрџЏ… <b>Р”РѕСЃСЏРіРЅРµРЅРЅСЏ:</b> {expert_eye}{community_voice}\n" if expert_eye or community_voice else ""

    status_text = "вњ… <b>РџР Р•РњР†РЈРњ</b>" if has_premium else "рџ”’ <b>Р‘Р°Р·РѕРІРёР№</b>"
    sponsor_badge = "рџЏ… <b>РЎРїРѕРЅСЃРѕСЂ РќРµС‚РёРєР°</b>\n" if user_data.get("is_sponsor") else ""

    text = (
        f"рџ‘¤ <b>РџСЂРѕС„С–Р»СЊ: {safe_name}</b> (@{safe_username})\n\n"
        f"рџ“… Р”Р°С‚Р° СЂРµС”СЃС‚СЂР°С†С–С—: <code>{safe_reg_date}</code>\n"
        f"рџ’і РЎС‚Р°С‚СѓСЃ: {status_text}\n"
        f"{sponsor_badge}"
        f"\nрџ“Љ <b>РўРІРѕСЏ СЃС‚Р°С‚РёСЃС‚РёРєР°:</b>\n"
        f"рџЋ¬ РџРµСЂРµРіР»СЏРЅСѓС‚Рѕ: <code>{safe_watched}</code>\n"
        f"рџЌї РЈ СЃРїРёСЃРєСѓ: <code>{safe_watchlist}</code>\n"
        f"в­ђ РћС†С–РЅРѕРє: <code>{safe_ratings}</code>\n"
        f"рџ“€ РЎРµСЂ. РѕС†С–РЅРєР°: <code>{safe_avg_rating}</code>\n"
        f"рџЏ† РњС–СЃС†Рµ РІ С‚РѕРїС–: <code>#{safe_top_position}</code>\n"
        f"рџЄ™ Р‘Р°Р»Рё: <code>{safe_points}</code>\n"
        f"{achievements_text}"
        f"\n<i>Р”СЏРєСѓСЋ, С‰Рѕ С‚Рё Р· РќРµС‚РёРєРѕРј!</i>"
    )

    notifs_on = bool(user_data.get("notifications_enabled", 1))
    markup = get_profile_keyboard(user_id, notifs_on)

    if isinstance(event, types.CallbackQuery):
        await event.message.edit_text(text, reply_markup=markup, parse_mode="HTML")
        await event.answer()
    else:
        await event.answer(text, reply_markup=markup, parse_mode="HTML")


@router.callback_query(F.data == "profile_notifications")
async def cb_notifications(callback: types.CallbackQuery):
    user_id = callback.from_user.id
    user = await db.get_user(user_id)
    if not user:
        await callback.answer("РџРѕРјРёР»РєР°: РєРѕСЂРёСЃС‚СѓРІР°С‡Р° РЅРµ Р·РЅР°Р№РґРµРЅРѕ.", show_alert=True)
        return

    notifs_on = bool(user.get("notifications_enabled", 1))

    new_val = 0 if notifs_on else 1
    await db.update_user(user_id, notifications_enabled=new_val)

    status = "СѓРІС–РјРєРЅРµРЅРѕ рџ””" if new_val else "РІРёРјРєРЅРµРЅРѕ рџ”•"
    await callback.answer(f"РЎРїРѕРІС–С‰РµРЅРЅСЏ {status}", show_alert=True)

    await show_profile(callback)

import logging
from typing import List, Dict, Any

from aiogram import Router, F, types
from aiogram.fsm.context import FSMContext
from aiogram.fsm.state import State, StatesGroup
from aiogram.types import InlineKeyboardButton, InlineKeyboardMarkup

from src.services.recommender import recommender_service
from src.services.tmdb import tmdb_service
from src.routers.movie import is_premium, show_movie_details
from src.config import config

router = Router()
logger = logging.getLogger(__name__)

class RecommendationStates(StatesGroup):
    VIEWING = State()


@router.callback_query(F.data == "menu_ai_rec")
async def cb_ai_recommendations(callback: types.CallbackQuery, state: FSMContext):
    """Handler for 'AI Recommendation' menu button."""
    user_id = callback.from_user.id
    
    # PREMIUM CHECK
    has_premium = await is_premium(user_id, callback.bot)
    if not has_premium:
        text = (
            "рџ”’ <b>РџРµСЂСЃРѕРЅР°Р»СЊРЅС– AI-СЂРµРєРѕРјРµРЅРґР°С†С–С— вЂ” С†Рµ Premium С„СѓРЅРєС†С–СЏ.</b>\n\n"
            "РќРµС‚РёРє РїСЂРѕР°РЅР°Р»С–Р·СѓС” С‚РІРѕС— СЃРјР°РєРё, РѕС†С–РЅРєРё С‚Р° РЅР°СЃС‚СЂС–Р№, С‰РѕР± РїС–РґС–Р±СЂР°С‚Рё С–РґРµР°Р»СЊРЅРµ РєС–РЅРѕ.\n\n"
            "РџС–РґРїРёС€РёСЃСЊ РЅР° РЅР°С€ РєР°РЅР°Р», С‰РѕР± СЂРѕР·Р±Р»РѕРєСѓРІР°С‚Рё С†РµР№ СЂРѕР·РґС–Р»!"
        )
        keyboard = InlineKeyboardMarkup(inline_keyboard=[
            [InlineKeyboardButton(text="рџ“ў РџС–РґРїРёСЃР°С‚РёСЃСЊ РЅР° РєР°РЅР°Р»", url=f"https://t.me/{config.CHANNEL_USERNAME.replace('@', '')}")],
            [InlineKeyboardButton(text="I РџС–РґРїРёСЃР°РІСЃСЏ! вњ…", callback_data="subscribe_check")],
            [InlineKeyboardButton(text="в¬…пёЏ Р’ РјРµРЅСЋ", callback_data="back_to_menu")]
        ])
        return await callback.message.answer(text, reply_markup=keyboard, parse_mode="HTML")

    await callback.answer()
    try:
        await callback.message.edit_text("рџ¤– <b>РќРµС‚РёРє РІРёРјРёРєР°С” Р»РѕРіС–РєСѓ С– РІРјРёРєР°С” С–РЅС‚СѓС—С†С–СЋ...</b>\nРђРЅР°Р»С–Р·СѓСЋ С‚РІРѕС— СЃРјР°РєРё, Р·Р°С‡РµРєР°Р№ С‚СЂС–С€РєРё.", parse_mode="HTML")
    except Exception:
        pass

    recs = await recommender_service.get_recommendations(user_id)

    if not recs:
        try:
            return await callback.message.edit_text(
                "рџ” РќРµС‚РёРє РїРѕРєРё РЅРµ Р·РјС–Рі РїС–РґС–Р±СЂР°С‚Рё РЅС–С‡РѕРіРѕ РѕСЃРѕР±Р»РёРІРѕРіРѕ. РЎРїСЂРѕР±СѓР№ РѕС†С–РЅРёС‚Рё Р±С–Р»СЊС€Рµ С„С–Р»СЊРјС–РІ!",
                reply_markup=InlineKeyboardMarkup(inline_keyboard=[[InlineKeyboardButton(text="в¬…пёЏ РњРµРЅСЋ", callback_data="back_to_menu")]])
            )
        except Exception:
            return

    await state.set_state(RecommendationStates.VIEWING)
    await state.update_data(ai_recs=recs, current_index=0)

    await show_recommendation_card(callback.message, recs[0], 0, len(recs))

async def show_recommendation_card(message: types.Message, movie: Dict[str, Any], index: int, total: int):
    """Displays a single recommendation card."""
    
    title = movie.get("title_ua")
    year = movie.get("year")
    tmdb_rating = movie.get("tmdb_rating", 0)
    why = movie.get("why", "")
    hook = movie.get("hook", "")
    netyk_says = movie.get("netyk_says", "")
    tmdb_id = movie.get("tmdb_id")
    poster_path = movie.get("poster_path")
    
    text = (
        f"рџ¤– <b>AI-РџРѕСЂР°РґР° ({index + 1}/{total})</b>\n\n"
        f"рџЋ¬ <b>{title}</b> ({year})\n"
        f"в­ђпёЏ Р РµР№С‚РёРЅРі TMDB: {tmdb_rating:.1f}/10\n\n"
        f"рџ’Ў <b>Р§РѕРјСѓ РІР°СЂС‚Рѕ РіР»СЏРЅСѓС‚Рё:</b>\n{why}\n\n"
        f"вњЁ <b>{hook}</b>\n\n"
        f"<i>{netyk_says}</i>"
    )
    
    keyboard = []
    # Action buttons
    action_row = []
    if tmdb_id:
        action_row.append(InlineKeyboardButton(text="рџЌї Р”Рѕ watchlist", callback_data=f"wl_add:{tmdb_id}"))
        action_row.append(InlineKeyboardButton(text="в­ђ РћС†С–РЅРёС‚Рё", callback_data=f"rate:{tmdb_id}"))
    keyboard.append(action_row)
    
    # Navigation row
    nav_row = []
    if index < total - 1:
        nav_row.append(InlineKeyboardButton(text="вћЎпёЏ РќР°СЃС‚СѓРїРЅР°", callback_data="next_ai_rec"))
    nav_row.append(InlineKeyboardButton(text="в¬…пёЏ РњРµРЅСЋ", callback_data="back_to_menu"))
    keyboard.append(nav_row)
    
    markup = InlineKeyboardMarkup(inline_keyboard=keyboard)
    
    if poster_path:
        photo_url = f"https://image.tmdb.org/t/p/w500{poster_path}"
        await message.answer_photo(photo=photo_url, caption=text, reply_markup=markup, parse_mode="HTML")
        try:
            await message.delete()
        except Exception:
            pass
    else:
        try:
            await message.edit_text(text, reply_markup=markup, parse_mode="HTML")
        except Exception as e:
            logger.warning(f"Failed to edit recs message: {e}")
            await message.answer(text, reply_markup=markup, parse_mode="HTML")

@router.callback_query(F.data == "next_ai_rec", RecommendationStates.VIEWING)
async def cb_next_ai_rec(callback: types.CallbackQuery, state: FSMContext):
    data = await state.get_data()
    recs = data.get("ai_recs", [])
    index = data.get("current_index", 0) + 1

    if index < len(recs):
        await state.update_data(current_index=index)
        await show_recommendation_card(callback.message, recs[index], index, len(recs))
        await callback.answer()
    else:
        await state.clear()
        await callback.answer("Р¦Рµ Р±СѓР»Р° РѕСЃС‚Р°РЅРЅСЏ РїРѕСЂР°РґР°!")

async def get_referral_link(bot, user_id: int) -> str:

import html
import logging
import json
import random
from aiogram import Router, F, types
from aiogram.types import InlineKeyboardButton, InlineKeyboardMarkup
from src.database.db import db
from src.services.tmdb import tmdb_service
from src.routers.movie import is_premium

router = Router()
logger = logging.getLogger(__name__)


@router.callback_query(F.data == "menu_swipe")
async def start_swipe_session(callback: types.CallbackQuery):
    user_id = callback.from_user.id
    if not await is_premium(user_id, callback.bot):
        return await callback.answer(
            "рџ”’ РЎРІР°Р№Рї-СЂРµР¶РёРј РґРѕСЃС‚СѓРїРЅРёР№ С‚С–Р»СЊРєРё РїС–РґРїРёСЃРЅРёРєР°Рј!", show_alert=True
        )
    if not await db.get_swipe_session(user_id):
        prefs = await db.get_user_preferences(user_id)
        if not prefs:
            prefs = {"genres": [], "period": "any"}
        genres = prefs.get("genres")
        if not genres: # If genres is empty or None, use default string
            genres = "Р‘РѕР№РѕРІРёРє,РљРѕРјРµРґС–СЏ"
        # period = prefs.get("period", "any") # 'period' is not used in save_swipe_session here
        await db.save_swipe_session(user_id, genres, 0, json.dumps([]))
    await show_next_swipe(callback)


async def show_next_swipe(callback: types.CallbackQuery):
    user_id = callback.from_user.id
    session = await db.get_swipe_session(user_id)
    if not session:
        return await callback.answer("РЎРµСЃС–СЋ РЅРµ Р·РЅР°Р№РґРµРЅРѕ.", show_alert=True)
        
    movies = await tmdb_service.get_popular_movies(page=random.randint(1, 10))
    swiped_ids = json.loads(session.get("session_data") or "[]")
    available = [m for m in movies if m.get("id") not in swiped_ids]

    if not available:
        return await callback.message.edit_text(
            "рџЋ‰ Р¤С–Р»СЊРјРё Р·Р°РєС–РЅС‡РёР»РёСЃСЊ! РЎРїСЂРѕР±СѓР№ РїС–Р·РЅС–С€Рµ.",
            reply_markup=InlineKeyboardMarkup(inline_keyboard=[
                [InlineKeyboardButton(text="в—ЂпёЏ РњРµРЅСЋ", callback_data="back_to_menu")],
            ]),
        )

    movie = available[0]
    overview = movie.get("overview") or ""

    safe_title = html.escape(movie.get('title', '?'))
    text = (
        f"рџѓЏ <b>РЎР’РђР™РџРђР›РљРђ РќР•РўРРљРђ</b>\n\n"
        f"рџЋ¬ <b>{safe_title}</b> ({(movie.get('release_date') or '0000')[:4]})\n"
        f"в­ђ Р РµР№С‚РёРЅРі: {movie.get('vote_average', 0)}\n\n"
        f"{html.escape(overview[:200])}{'...' if len(overview) > 200 else ''}"
    )
    keyboard = InlineKeyboardMarkup(inline_keyboard=[
        [
            InlineKeyboardButton(text="рџ‘Ћ", callback_data=f"swipe_dislike:{movie['id']}"),
            InlineKeyboardButton(text="рџ‘Ќ", callback_data=f"swipe_like:{movie['id']}"),
        ],
        [InlineKeyboardButton(text="рџ“‹ Р”РµС‚Р°Р»С–", callback_data=f"movie_id:{movie['id']}")],
        [InlineKeyboardButton(text="рџ›‘ Р—Р°РІРµСЂС€РёС‚Рё", callback_data="back_to_menu")],
    ])

    try:
        await callback.message.delete()
    except Exception:
        pass

    try:
        poster_url = await tmdb_service.get_poster_url(movie.get("poster_path"))
        if poster_url:
            await callback.message.answer_photo(
                poster_url, caption=text, reply_markup=keyboard, parse_mode="HTML"
            )
        else:
            await callback.message.answer(text, reply_markup=keyboard, parse_mode="HTML")
    except Exception as e:
        logger.error(f"Error showing swipe: {e}")
        await callback.message.answer("РџРѕРјРёР»РєР° РІС–РґРѕР±СЂР°Р¶РµРЅРЅСЏ С„С–Р»СЊРјСѓ.")


@router.callback_query(F.data.startswith("swipe_"))
async def handle_swipe(callback: types.CallbackQuery):
    action, tmdb_id_str = callback.data.split(":")
    tmdb_id = int(tmdb_id_str)
    user_id = callback.from_user.id

    session = await db.get_swipe_session(user_id)
    if not session:
        # Assuming 'genres' is a string, 'last_movie_id' is int, 'session_data' is JSON string
        # The original save_swipe_session takes (user_id, genres, last_movie_id, session_data)
        # The provided snippet for save_swipe_session(user_id, "{}", datetime.now().isoformat())
        # does not match the signature of the existing save_swipe_session.
        # I will use default values that match the existing signature.
        await db.save_swipe_session(user_id, "Р‘РѕР№РѕРІРёРє,РљРѕРјРµРґС–СЏ", 0, json.dumps([]))
        session = await db.get_swipe_session(user_id)

    if not session:
        # If session is still None after attempting to create it, something is wrong.
        # The original code uses callback.message.edit_text or callback.answer.
        # Using callback.answer for consistency.
        await callback.answer("РџРѕРјРёР»РєР° РїСЂРё СЃС‚РІРѕСЂРµРЅРЅС– СЃРµСЃС–С—.", show_alert=True)
        return

    # The original code uses 'session_data' key. The provided snippet uses 'history'.
    # Sticking to 'session_data' as per the existing code.
    swiped = json.loads(session.get("session_data") or "[]")
    if tmdb_id not in swiped:
        swiped.append(tmdb_id)
    await db.save_swipe_session(
        user_id, session.get("genres", ""), tmdb_id, json.dumps(swiped)
    )

    if action == "swipe_like":
        try:
            movie = await tmdb_service.get_movie_details(tmdb_id)
            title = movie.get("title", "Р¤С–Р»СЊРј")
            await db.add_to_watchlist(user_id, tmdb_id, title)
            await callback.answer(f"вќ¤пёЏ '{title}' Сѓ СЃРїРёСЃРєСѓ!")
        except Exception as e:
            logger.error(f"Error in swipe_like: {e}")
            await callback.answer("вљ пёЏ РџРѕРјРёР»РєР° РґРѕРґР°РІР°РЅРЅСЏ.", show_alert=True)
    else:
        await callback.answer("рџ‘Ћ РџСЂРѕРїСѓС‰РµРЅРѕ")

    await show_next_swipe(callback)

import logging

async def _render_watchlist(message: types.Message, user_id: int, status: str):
    items = await db.get_watchlist(user_id, status)
    status_map = {"want": "рџ‘Ђ РҐРѕС‡Сѓ РґРёРІРёС‚РёСЃСЊ", "watching": "в–¶пёЏ Р”РёРІР»СЋСЃСЊ Р·Р°СЂР°Р·", "watched": "вњ… РџРµСЂРµРіР»СЏРЅСѓС‚Рѕ"}
    label = status_map.get(status, "РњС–Р№ СЃРїРёСЃРѕРє")
    text = f"рџ“‚ *{label}* ({len(items)})\n\n"
    if not items:
        text += "_РўСѓС‚ РїРѕРєРё РїРѕСЂРѕР¶РЅСЊРѕ..._"

    tabs = [
        InlineKeyboardButton(text="вЂў рџ‘Ђ РҐРѕС‡Сѓ вЂў" if status=="want" else "рџ‘Ђ РҐРѕС‡Сѓ", callback_data="wl_tab:want"),
        InlineKeyboardButton(text="вЂў в–¶пёЏ Р”РёРІР»СЋСЃСЊ вЂў" if status=="watching" else "в–¶пёЏ Р”РёРІР»СЋСЃСЊ", callback_data="wl_tab:watching"),
        InlineKeyboardButton(text="вЂў вњ… Р“РѕС‚РѕРІРѕ вЂў" if status=="watched" else "вњ… Р“РѕС‚РѕРІРѕ", callback_data="wl_tab:watched"),
    ]
    keyboard = [tabs]
    for item in items[:10]:
        keyboard.append([InlineKeyboardButton(text=item["title_ua"], callback_data=f"wl_manage:{item['tmdb_id']}")])
    keyboard.append([InlineKeyboardButton(text="в—ЂпёЏ РњРµРЅСЋ", callback_data="back_to_menu")])
    try:
        await message.edit_text(text, reply_markup=InlineKeyboardMarkup(inline_keyboard=keyboard), parse_mode="Markdown")
    except Exception:
        await message.answer(text, reply_markup=InlineKeyboardMarkup(inline_keyboard=keyboard), parse_mode="Markdown")

    keyboard = [
        [InlineKeyboardButton(text="рџ“‹ Р”РµС‚Р°Р»С–", callback_data=f"movie_id:{tmdb_id}")],
        [InlineKeyboardButton(text="рџ‘Ђ РҐРѕС‡Сѓ", callback_data=f"wl_set:{tmdb_id}:want"),
         InlineKeyboardButton(text="в–¶пёЏ Р”РёРІР»СЋСЃСЊ", callback_data=f"wl_set:{tmdb_id}:watching"),
         InlineKeyboardButton(text="вњ… Р“РѕС‚РѕРІРѕ", callback_data=f"wl_set:{tmdb_id}:watched")],
        [InlineKeyboardButton(text="рџ—‘ Р’РёРґР°Р»РёС‚Рё", callback_data=f"wl_del:{tmdb_id}")],
        [InlineKeyboardButton(text="в—ЂпёЏ Р”Рѕ СЃРїРёСЃРєСѓ", callback_data=f"wl_tab:{item['status']}")],
    ]
    try:
        await message.edit_text(text, reply_markup=InlineKeyboardMarkup(inline_keyboard=keyboard), parse_mode="Markdown")
    except Exception:
        await message.answer(text, reply_markup=InlineKeyboardMarkup(inline_keyboard=keyboard), parse_mode="Markdown")

===== G:\NeNetflixBot\src\services\__init__.py =====
# РџР°РєРµС‚ services


===== G:\NeNetflixBot\src\services\ai.py =====
import asyncio
import json
import logging
from typing import Any, Dict, Optional, Union

from google import genai
from groq import AsyncGroq

from src.config import config

logger = logging.getLogger(__name__)


class AIService:
    def __init__(self):
        self.groq_client = AsyncGroq(api_key=config.GROQ_API_KEY, timeout=8.0)
        self.gemini_client = genai.Client(api_key=config.GEMINI_API_KEY)

    async def ask(
        self, prompt: str, expect_json: bool = True
    ) -> Union[Dict[str, Any], str, None]:
        """
        Main method to get AI response.
        First tries Groq (Llama 3.3 70B), then falls back to Gemini 2.0 Flash.
        """
        try:
            logger.info("Requesting Groq Llama 3.3...")
            response = await self._ask_groq(prompt, expect_json)
            if response is not None:
                logger.info("Success using Groq")
                return response
        except Exception as e:
            logger.error(f"Groq API error: {e}")

        try:
            logger.info("Requesting Gemini 2.0 Flash (fallback)...")
            response = await self._ask_gemini(prompt, expect_json)
            if response is not None:
                logger.info("Success using Gemini fallback")
                return response
        except Exception as e:
            logger.error(f"Gemini API error: {e}")

        logger.error("Both AI services failed.")
        return None

    async def _ask_groq(self, prompt: str, expect_json: bool) -> Any:
        response_format = {"type": "json_object"} if expect_json else None

        chat_completion = await self.groq_client.chat.completions.create(
            messages=[{"role": "user", "content": prompt}],
            model="llama-3.3-70b-versatile",
            response_format=response_format,
        )
        content = chat_completion.choices[0].message.content
        return self._parse_json(content) if expect_json else content

    async def _ask_gemini(self, prompt: str, expect_json: bool) -> Any:
        if expect_json and "JSON" not in prompt:
            prompt += "\n\nProvide response in strict JSON format."

        response = await asyncio.to_thread(
            self.gemini_client.models.generate_content,
            model="gemini-1.5-flash",
            contents=prompt,
        )
        content = response.text

        if expect_json:
            content = content.strip()
            if content.startswith("```json"):
                content = content[7:]
            if content.startswith("```"):
                content = content[3:]
            if content.endswith("```"):
                content = content[:-3]
            content = content.strip()

        return self._parse_json(content) if expect_json else content

    def _parse_json(self, content: str) -> Optional[Dict[str, Any]]:
        try:
            return json.loads(content)
        except json.JSONDecodeError as e:
            logger.error(f"Failed to parse JSON: {e}. Content: {content}")
            return None


# Global instance
ai_service = AIService()

===== G:\NeNetflixBot\src\services\image_generator.py =====
import os
import logging
from PIL import Image, ImageDraw, ImageFont, ImageFilter

logger = logging.getLogger(__name__)

class ImageGenerator:
    def __init__(self, font_path: str = "src/assets/fonts/font.ttf"):
        self.font_path = font_path
        self.width = 1080
        self.height = 1080
        self.bg_color = (15, 15, 15)  # Dark Netflix-style bg
        self.accent_color = (229, 9, 20)  # Netflix Red

    def create_quote_card(self, text: str, author: str, output_path: str = "src/assets/temp_quote.png") -> str:
        """
        Generates a 1080x1080 quote card with gradients and styling.
        """
        # Create base image
        img = Image.new('RGB', (self.width, self.height), color=self.bg_color)
        draw = ImageDraw.Draw(img)

        # Add subtle gradient or background decoration
        for i in range(self.height):
            # Very subtle vertical gradient
            r = max(10, 15 - int(i / 100))
            draw.line([(0, i), (self.width, i)], fill=(r, 15, 15))

        # Accent line at the top
        draw.rectangle([0, 0, self.width, 10], fill=self.accent_color)

        # Load fonts
        try:
            quote_font = ImageFont.truetype(self.font_path, 60)
            author_font = ImageFont.truetype(self.font_path, 40)
            logo_font = ImageFont.truetype(self.font_path, 30)
        except OSError:
            logger.warning(f"Font not found at {self.font_path}. Using default font.")
            quote_font = ImageFont.load_default()
            author_font = ImageFont.load_default()
            logo_font = ImageFont.load_default()

        # Wrap text
        wrapped_text = self._wrap_text(text, quote_font, self.width - 200)
        
        # Calculate positions
        # Center quote
        total_text_height = self._get_text_height(wrapped_text, quote_font)
        y_start = (self.height - total_text_height) // 2

        # Draw quote
        current_y = y_start
        for line in wrapped_text:
            # Get line width for centering
            bbox = draw.textbbox((0, 0), line, font=quote_font)
            line_width = bbox[2] - bbox[0]
            draw.text(((self.width - line_width) // 2, current_y), line, font=quote_font, fill=(255, 255, 255))
            current_y += (bbox[3] - bbox[1]) + 20

        # Draw author
        author_text = f"вЂ” {author}"
        bbox_author = draw.textbbox((0, 0), author_text, font=author_font)
        author_width = bbox_author[2] - bbox_author[0]
        draw.text(((self.width - author_width) // 2, current_y + 40), author_text, font=author_font, fill=self.accent_color)

        # Draw "NeNetflix Bot" watermark at bottom
        watermark = "NeNetflix Bot рџЋ¬"
        bbox_wm = draw.textbbox((0, 0), watermark, font=logo_font)
        wm_width = bbox_wm[2] - bbox_wm[0]
        draw.text(((self.width - wm_width) // 2, self.height - 100), watermark, font=logo_font, fill=(100, 100, 100))

        # Save
        os.makedirs(os.path.dirname(output_path), exist_ok=True)
        img.save(output_path)
        return output_path

    def _wrap_text(self, text, font, max_width):
        lines = []
        words = text.split()
        current_line = []

        for word in words:
            test_line = " ".join(current_line + [word])
            # Use textbbox instead of textsize (deprecated in Pillow 10)
            temp_img = Image.new('RGB', (1, 1))
            temp_draw = ImageDraw.Draw(temp_img)
            bbox = temp_draw.textbbox((0, 0), test_line, font=font)
            width = bbox[2] - bbox[0]
            
            if width <= max_width:
                current_line.append(word)
            else:
                lines.append(" ".join(current_line))
                current_line = [word]
        
        lines.append(" ".join(current_line))
        return lines

    def _get_text_height(self, lines, font):
        total_height = 0
        temp_img = Image.new('RGB', (1, 1))
        temp_draw = ImageDraw.Draw(temp_img)
        for line in lines:
            bbox = temp_draw.textbbox((0, 0), line, font=font)
            total_height += (bbox[3] - bbox[1]) + 20
        return total_height - 20 # Remove last spacing

image_generator = ImageGenerator()

  "visual_mood": "dark Р°Р±Рѕ warm Р°Р±Рѕ epic Р°Р±Рѕ melancholic Р°Р±Рѕ funny"

Р’С–РґРїРѕРІС–РґР°Р№ РўР†Р›Р¬РљР РІР°Р»С–РґРЅРёРј JSON Р±РµР· РґРѕРґР°С‚РєРѕРІРѕРіРѕ С‚РµРєСЃС‚Сѓ.

HIDDEN_GEM_PROMPT = """

  "body": "200-250 СЃРёРјРІРѕР»С–РІ. Р‘Р•Р— РЎРџРћР™Р›Р•Р Р†Р’. РђС‚РјРѕСЃС„РµСЂР°, РЅРµ СЃСЋР¶РµС‚.",

  "not_for_who": "РљРѕРјСѓ РќР• РІР°СЂС‚Рѕ РґРёРІРёС‚РёСЃСЊ. Р§РµСЃРЅРѕ. 1 РєРѕСЂРѕС‚РєРµ СЂРµС‡РµРЅРЅСЏ.",
  "signature": "вЂ” РќРµС‚РёРє [РѕСЃРѕР±РёСЃС‚Р° РґСѓРјРєР°]. Р”Рѕ 15 СЃР»С–РІ. Р— С…Р°СЂР°РєС‚РµСЂРѕРј."
}}

Р’С–РґРїРѕРІС–РґР°Р№ РўР†Р›Р¬РљР РІР°Р»С–РґРЅРёРј JSON Р±РµР· РґРѕРґР°С‚РєРѕРІРѕРіРѕ С‚РµРєСЃС‚Сѓ.
"""

WEEKLY_SUMMARY_PROMPT = """
РўРё вЂ” РќРµС‚РёРє, РІРµРґСѓС‡РёР№ С‰РѕС‚РёР¶РЅРµРІРёС… РїС–РґСЃСѓРјРєС–РІ.

  "highlight": "РќР°Р№СЏСЃРєСЂР°РІС–С€РёР№ РјРѕРјРµРЅС‚. 1 РєРѕСЂРѕС‚РєРµ СЂРµС‡РµРЅРЅСЏ.",
  "cta": "Р—Р°РєР»РёРє РїС–РґРїРёСЃР°С‚Рё РґСЂСѓРіР°. РќРµСЃС‚Р°РЅРґР°СЂС‚РЅРёР№, РЅРµ Р±Р°РЅР°Р»СЊРЅРёР№. Р”Рѕ 80 СЃРёРјРІРѕР»С–РІ.",

===== G:\NeNetflixBot\src\services\recommender.py =====
import asyncio
import logging
from typing import List, Dict, Any, Optional

from src.database.db import db
from src.services.ai import ai_service
from src.services.tmdb import tmdb_service
from src.services.prompts import RECOMMENDATION_PROMPT

logger = logging.getLogger(__name__)

class RecommenderService:
    async def get_recommendations(self, user_id: int, mood: str = "СЃРїРѕРєС–Р№РЅРёР№") -> List[Dict[str, Any]]:
        """Generates AI recommendations based on user history and preferences."""
        
        # 1. Collect User Context
        prefs = await db.get_user_preferences(user_id)
        if not prefs:
            return [] # Should not happen if onboarding is done
            
        ratings_summary = await db.get_user_ratings_summary(user_id)
        watched_titles = await db.get_watched_titles(user_id)
        
        # 2. Prepare Prompt
        prompt = RECOMMENDATION_PROMPT.format(
            genres=prefs.get("genres", "Р±СѓРґСЊ-СЏРєС–"),
            watched_titles=", ".join(watched_titles) if watched_titles else "РЅС–С‡РѕРіРѕ",
            avg_rating=ratings_summary.get("avg", 0),
            liked_titles=", ".join(ratings_summary.get("liked", [])) if ratings_summary.get("liked") else "РЅРµРјР°С”",
            disliked_titles=", ".join(ratings_summary.get("disliked", [])) if ratings_summary.get("disliked") else "РЅРµРјР°С”",
            fav_decade=prefs.get("fav_period", "Р±СѓРґСЊ-СЏРєРёР№"),
            mood=mood
        )
        
        # 3. Get AI Response
        ai_response = await ai_service.ask(prompt, expect_json=True)
        if not ai_response or "recommendations" not in ai_response:
            logger.error("AI failed to provide recommendations")
            return []
            
        async def enrich_rec(rec):
            # 4. Enrich with TMDB data (ID and Poster)
            search_results = await tmdb_service.search_movies(rec["title"], limit=1)
            if not search_results:
                # Try with title_ua
                search_results = await tmdb_service.search_movies(rec["title_ua"], limit=1)
            
            if search_results:
                movie_data = search_results[0]
                rec["tmdb_id"] = movie_data.get("id")
                rec["poster_path"] = movie_data.get("poster_path")
                rec["tmdb_rating"] = movie_data.get("vote_average")
            else:
                rec["tmdb_id"] = None
                rec["poster_path"] = None
                rec["tmdb_rating"] = 0
            return rec

        tasks = [enrich_rec(rec) for rec in ai_response["recommendations"]]
        final_recs = await asyncio.gather(*tasks)
            
        return final_recs

recommender_service = RecommenderService()


===== G:\NeNetflixBot\src\services\scheduler.py =====
import logging
import asyncio
import random
import json
from apscheduler.schedulers.asyncio import AsyncIOScheduler
from aiogram import Bot

from src.config import config
from src.database.db import db
from src.services.ai import ai_service
from src.services.tmdb import tmdb_service
from src.services.prompts import (
    MORNING_POST_PROMPT,
    QUOTE_OF_DAY_PROMPT,
    HIDDEN_GEM_PROMPT,
    DAILY_PICKS_PROMPT,
    CONTROVERSIAL_POST_PROMPT,
    WEEKLY_SUMMARY_PROMPT,
)
from src.services.image_generator import image_generator

logger = logging.getLogger(__name__)


class ChannelScheduler:
    def __init__(self, bot: Bot):
        self.bot = bot
        self.scheduler = AsyncIOScheduler(timezone="Europe/Kyiv")

    def start(self):
        # Mon-Fri 09:00 вЂ” Morning movie post
        self.scheduler.add_job(self.post_morning_movie, "cron", hour=9, minute=0)

        # Every day 13:00 вЂ” Quote of the day (Pillow card)
        self.scheduler.add_job(self.post_quote_of_day, "cron", hour=13, minute=0)

        # Tue & Thu 18:00 вЂ” Controversial hot take (overrated / underrated)
        self.scheduler.add_job(self.post_controversial, "cron", day_of_week="tue,thu", hour=18, minute=0)

        # Fri 17:00 вЂ” Hidden gem
        self.scheduler.add_job(self.post_hidden_gem, "cron", day_of_week="fri", hour=17, minute=0)

        # Every day 21:00 вЂ” Daily picks
        self.scheduler.add_job(self.post_daily_picks, "cron", hour=21, minute=0)

        # Sun 12:00 вЂ” Weekly summary
        self.scheduler.add_job(self.post_weekly_summary, "cron", day_of_week="sun", hour=12, minute=0)

        self.scheduler.start()
        logger.info("Channel Scheduler started with 6 jobs.")

    # в”Ђв”Ђ 1. Morning Movie (09:00 daily) в”Ђв”Ђв”Ђв”Ђв”Ђв”Ђв”Ђв”Ђв”Ђв”Ђв”Ђв”Ђв”Ђв”Ђв”Ђв”Ђв”Ђв”Ђв”Ђв”Ђв”Ђв”Ђв”Ђв”Ђв”Ђ

    async def post_morning_movie(self):
        try:
            movies = await tmdb_service.get_trending()
            if not movies:
                return logger.warning("post_morning_movie: no trending movies")

            movie = movies[0]
            prompt = MORNING_POST_PROMPT.format(
                title=movie.get('title', 'РќРµРІС–РґРѕРјРёР№ С„С–Р»СЊРј'),
                year=(movie.get('release_date') or '0000')[:4],
                genres=movie.get('genre_ids', []),
                rating=movie.get('vote_average', 0),
                overview=movie.get('overview') or 'РћРїРёСЃ РІС–РґСЃСѓС‚РЅС–Р№.'
            )

            res = await ai_service.ask(prompt, expect_json=True)
            if not res or 'post' not in res or 'signature' not in res:
                return logger.warning("post_morning_movie: incomplete AI response")

            text = f"{res['post']}\n\n{res['signature']}"
            bot_msg = await self.bot.send_message(chat_id=config.CHANNEL_ID, text=text)
            await db.save_channel_post("morning", res['post'][:100], text, movie.get('id'), bot_msg.message_id)
            logger.info("Morning post sent.")
        except Exception as e:
            logger.error(f"post_morning_movie error: {e}", exc_info=True)

    # в”Ђв”Ђ 2. Quote of the Day (13:00 daily) в”Ђв”Ђв”Ђв”Ђв”Ђв”Ђв”Ђв”Ђв”Ђв”Ђв”Ђв”Ђв”Ђв”Ђв”Ђв”Ђв”Ђв”Ђв”Ђв”Ђв”Ђв”Ђ

    async def post_quote_of_day(self):
        try:
            res = await ai_service.ask(QUOTE_OF_DAY_PROMPT, expect_json=True)
            if not res or 'quote_ua' not in res or 'film' not in res:
                return logger.warning("post_quote_of_day: incomplete AI response")

            img_path = image_generator.create_quote_card(
                res['quote_ua'],
                res.get('character') or res['film']
            )

            # FIX: single * for Markdown v1 (was **)
            caption = (
                f"рџЋ¬ *Р¦РёС‚Р°С‚Р° РґРЅСЏ*\n\n"
                f"_{res['quote_ua']}_\n\n"
                f"рџ“Њ {res['film']} ({res.get('year', '')})\n"
                f"рџ’Ў {res.get('why_today', '')}\n\n"
                f"@{config.CHANNEL_USERNAME.replace('@', '')}"
            )

            from aiogram.types import FSInputFile
            bot_msg = await self.bot.send_photo(
                chat_id=config.CHANNEL_ID,
                photo=FSInputFile(img_path),
                caption=caption,
                parse_mode="Markdown"
            )
            await db.save_channel_post("quote", res['quote_ua'][:100], caption, None, bot_msg.message_id)
            logger.info("Quote post sent.")
        except Exception as e:
            logger.error(f"post_quote_of_day error: {e}", exc_info=True)

    # в”Ђв”Ђ 3. Controversial Hot Take (Tue & Thu 18:00) в”Ђв”Ђв”Ђв”Ђв”Ђв”Ђв”Ђв”Ђв”Ђв”Ђв”Ђв”Ђ

    async def post_controversial(self):
        """Overrated or underrated movie вЂ” provokes discussion."""
        try:
            movies = await tmdb_service.get_popular_movies(page=random.randint(1, 5))
            if not movies:
                return logger.warning("post_controversial: no movies")

            movie = random.choice(movies)
            tmdb_rating = movie.get("vote_average", 5)

            # High-rated = potentially overrated, low-rated = potentially underrated
            post_type = "overrated" if tmdb_rating >= 7.5 else "underrated"

            prompt = CONTROVERSIAL_POST_PROMPT.format(
                title=movie.get("title", "РќРµРІС–РґРѕРјРёР№ С„С–Р»СЊРј"),
                year=(movie.get("release_date") or "0000")[:4],
                imdb_rating=tmdb_rating,
                post_type=post_type
            )

            res = await ai_service.ask(prompt, expect_json=True)
            if not res or "headline" not in res or "argument" not in res:
                return logger.warning("post_controversial: incomplete AI response")

            type_emoji = "рџ“‰" if post_type == "overrated" else "рџ“€"
            type_label = "РџР•Р Р•РћР¦Р†РќР•РќРћ" if post_type == "overrated" else "РќР•Р”РћРћР¦Р†РќР•РќРћ"

            # FIX: single * for Markdown v1 (was **)
            text = (
                f"{type_emoji} *{type_label}*\n\n"
                f"рџ”Ґ *{res['headline']}*\n\n"
                f"{res['argument']}\n\n"
                f"рџ¤” {res.get('counterpoint', '')}\n\n"
                f"рџ’¬ {res.get('question', '')}\n\n"
                f"{res.get('signature', 'вЂ” РќРµС‚РёРє')}"
            )

            poster_url = await tmdb_service.get_poster_url(movie.get("poster_path"))
            if poster_url:
                bot_msg = await self.bot.send_photo(
                    chat_id=config.CHANNEL_ID,
                    photo=poster_url,
                    caption=text,
                    parse_mode="Markdown"
                )
            else:
                bot_msg = await self.bot.send_message(
                    chat_id=config.CHANNEL_ID,
                    text=text,
                    parse_mode="Markdown"
                )

            await db.save_channel_post("controversial", res["headline"][:100], text, movie.get("id"), bot_msg.message_id)
            logger.info(f"Controversial post sent: {post_type}")
        except Exception as e:
            logger.error(f"post_controversial error: {e}", exc_info=True)

    # в”Ђв”Ђ 4. Hidden Gem (Fri 17:00) в”Ђв”Ђв”Ђв”Ђв”Ђв”Ђв”Ђв”Ђв”Ђв”Ђв”Ђв”Ђв”Ђв”Ђв”Ђв”Ђв”Ђв”Ђв”Ђв”Ђв”Ђв”Ђв”Ђв”Ђв”Ђв”Ђв”Ђв”Ђв”Ђв”Ђ

    async def post_hidden_gem(self):
        try:
            movies = await tmdb_service.get_popular_movies(page=random.randint(5, 15))
            if not movies:
                return logger.warning("post_hidden_gem: no movies")

            movie = random.choice(movies)
            details = await tmdb_service.get_movie_details(movie['id'])

            credits_data = await tmdb_service.get_movie_credits(movie['id'])
            director = "РќРµРІС–РґРѕРјРёР№"
            for crew in credits_data.get('crew', []):
                if crew.get('job') == 'Director':
                    director = crew['name']
                    break

            prompt = HIDDEN_GEM_PROMPT.format(
                title=movie.get('title', 'РќРµРІС–РґРѕРјРёР№ С„С–Р»СЊРј'),
                year=(movie.get('release_date') or '0000')[:4],
                genres=", ".join([g['name'] for g in details.get('genres', [])]),
                director=director,
                rating=movie.get('vote_average', 0),
                overview=movie.get('overview') or 'РћРїРёСЃ РІС–РґСЃСѓС‚РЅС–Р№.'
            )

            res = await ai_service.ask(prompt, expect_json=True)
            if not res or 'hook' not in res or 'body' not in res:
                return logger.warning("post_hidden_gem: incomplete AI response")

            # FIX: single * for Markdown v1 (was **)
            text = (
                f"рџ’Ћ *РџСЂРёС…РѕРІР°РЅР° РїРµСЂР»РёРЅР°*\n\n"
                f"*{res['hook']}*\n\n"
                f"{res['body']}\n\n"
                f"вњЁ *Р¦С–РєР°РІР° РґРµС‚Р°Р»СЊ:* {res.get('best_moment', '')}\n"
                f"рџљ« *РќРµ РґР»СЏ С‚РёС…...* {res.get('not_for_who', '')}\n\n"
                f"{res.get('signature', 'вЂ” РќРµС‚РёРє')}"
            )

            poster_url = await tmdb_service.get_poster_url(movie.get('poster_path'))
            if poster_url:
                bot_msg = await self.bot.send_photo(
                    chat_id=config.CHANNEL_ID, photo=poster_url,
                    caption=text, parse_mode="Markdown"
                )
            else:
                bot_msg = await self.bot.send_message(
                    chat_id=config.CHANNEL_ID, text=text, parse_mode="Markdown"
                )

            await db.save_channel_post("hidden_gem", res['hook'][:100], text, movie.get('id'), bot_msg.message_id)
            logger.info("Hidden gem post sent.")
        except Exception as e:
            logger.error(f"post_hidden_gem error: {e}", exc_info=True)

    # в”Ђв”Ђ 5. Daily Picks (21:00 daily) в”Ђв”Ђв”Ђв”Ђв”Ђв”Ђв”Ђв”Ђв”Ђв”Ђв”Ђв”Ђв”Ђв”Ђв”Ђв”Ђв”Ђв”Ђв”Ђв”Ђв”Ђв”Ђв”Ђв”Ђв”Ђв”Ђв”Ђ

    async def post_daily_picks(self):
        try:
            popular_movies = await tmdb_service.get_popular(page=1)
            if not popular_movies:
                return logger.warning("post_daily_picks: no popular movies")

            movies_for_ai = [
                {
                    "id": m.get("id"),
                    "title": m.get("title"),
                    "year": (m.get("release_date") or "")[:4],
                    "overview": (m.get("overview") or "")[:100]
                }
                for m in popular_movies[:15]
            ]

            prompt = DAILY_PICKS_PROMPT.format(
                tmdb_movies_json=json.dumps(movies_for_ai, ensure_ascii=False)
            )
            content = await ai_service.ask(prompt, expect_json=True)

            if not content or 'intro' not in content or 'films' not in content:
                return logger.warning("post_daily_picks: AI returned incomplete content")

            # FIX: single * for Markdown v1 (was **)
            text = f"рџЋЃ *Р”РѕР±С–СЂРєР° РґРЅСЏ РІС–Рґ РќРµС‚РёРєР°*\n\n{content['intro']}\n\n"
            for film in content.get('films', []):
                text += f"{film.get('emoji', 'рџЋ¬')} *{film.get('title_ua', 'Р¤С–Р»СЊРј')}* вЂ” {film.get('pitch', '')}\n\n"

            outro = content.get('outro', '')
            if outro:
                text += f"{outro}\n\n"
            text += f"рџЋ¬ @{config.CHANNEL_USERNAME.replace('@', '')}"

            bot_msg = await self.bot.send_message(
                chat_id=config.CHANNEL_ID, text=text, parse_mode="Markdown"
            )
            await db.save_channel_post("daily_picks", content['intro'][:100], text, None, bot_msg.message_id)
            logger.info("Daily picks post sent to channel.")
        except Exception as e:
            logger.error(f"post_daily_picks error: {e}", exc_info=True)

    # в”Ђв”Ђ 6. Weekly Summary (Sun 12:00) в”Ђв”Ђв”Ђв”Ђв”Ђв”Ђв”Ђв”Ђв”Ђв”Ђв”Ђв”Ђв”Ђв”Ђв”Ђв”Ђв”Ђв”Ђв”Ђв”Ђв”Ђв”Ђв”Ђв”Ђв”Ђв”Ђ

    async def post_weekly_summary(self):
        """Weekly recap with stats, highlights and CTA."""
        try:
            stats = await db.get_weekly_stats()

            prompt = WEEKLY_SUMMARY_PROMPT.format(
                films_count=stats["films_count"],
                poll_winner=stats["poll_winner"],
                new_subs=stats["new_subs"],
                top_user=stats["top_user"]
            )

            res = await ai_service.ask(prompt, expect_json=True)
            if not res or "summary" not in res:
                return logger.warning("post_weekly_summary: incomplete AI response")

            # FIX: single * for Markdown v1 (was **)
            text = (
                f"рџ“Љ *РџС–РґСЃСѓРјРєРё С‚РёР¶РЅСЏ РІС–Рґ РќРµС‚РёРєР°*\n\n"
                f"{res['summary']}\n\n"
                f"вњЁ {res.get('highlight', '')}\n\n"
                f"{res.get('cta', '')}\n\n"
                f"{res.get('signature', 'вЂ” РќРµС‚РёРє')}\n\n"
                f"рџЋ¬ @{config.CHANNEL_USERNAME.replace('@', '')}"
            )

            bot_msg = await self.bot.send_message(
                chat_id=config.CHANNEL_ID,
                text=text,
                parse_mode="Markdown"
            )
            await db.save_channel_post("weekly_summary", res["summary"][:100], text, None, bot_msg.message_id)
            logger.info("Weekly summary post sent.")
        except Exception as e:
            logger.error(f"post_weekly_summary error: {e}", exc_info=True)

===== G:\NeNetflixBot\src\services\tmdb.py =====
import aiohttp
import logging
from typing import Any, Dict, List, Optional
from src.config import config

logger = logging.getLogger(__name__)


class TMDBService:
    BASE_URL = "https://api.themoviedb.org/3"
    IMAGE_BASE_URL = "https://image.tmdb.org/t/p/w500"

    def __init__(self, api_key: str):
        self.api_key = api_key
        self._session: aiohttp.ClientSession | None = None

    async def _get_session(self) -> aiohttp.ClientSession:
        if self._session is None or self._session.closed:
            self._session = aiohttp.ClientSession()
        return self._session

    async def close(self):
        """Graceful shutdown вЂ” close persistent HTTP session."""
        if self._session and not self._session.closed:
            await self._session.close()
            logger.info("TMDB session closed.")

    async def _get(self, endpoint: str, params: Optional[Dict[str, Any]] = None) -> Dict[str, Any]:
        if params is None:
            params = {}
        params["api_key"] = self.api_key
        params["language"] = "uk-UA"

        session = await self._get_session()
        try:
            async with session.get(f"{self.BASE_URL}{endpoint}", params=params) as response:
                if response.status == 200:
                    return await response.json()
                else:
                    logger.error(f"TMDB API error: {response.status} for {endpoint}")
                    if params.get("language") == "uk-UA":
                        params["language"] = "en-US"
                        async with session.get(f"{self.BASE_URL}{endpoint}", params=params) as en_response:
                            return await en_response.json()
                    return {}
        except Exception as e:
            logger.error(f"TMDB request failed: {e}")
            return {}

    async def search_movies(self, query: str, limit: int = 10) -> List[Dict[str, Any]]:
        data = await self._get("/search/movie", {"query": query})
        results = data.get("results", [])
        return results[:limit]

    async def get_movie_details(self, movie_id: int) -> Dict[str, Any]:
        return await self._get(f"/movie/{movie_id}")

    async def get_movie_credits(self, movie_id: int) -> Dict[str, Any]:
        return await self._get(f"/movie/{movie_id}/credits")

    async def get_similar_movies(self, movie_id: int) -> List[Dict[str, Any]]:
        data = await self._get(f"/movie/{movie_id}/similar")
        return data.get("results", [])

    async def get_trending(self, time_window: str = "week") -> List[Dict[str, Any]]:
        data = await self._get(f"/trending/movie/{time_window}")
        return data.get("results", [])

    async def get_popular(self, page: int = 1) -> List[Dict[str, Any]]:
        data = await self._get("/movie/popular", {"page": page})
        return data.get("results", [])

    async def get_popular_movies(self, page: int = 1) -> List[Dict[str, Any]]:
        """Alias for get_popular вЂ” for compatibility."""
        return await self.get_popular(page=page)

    def get_poster_url(self, path: Optional[str]) -> Optional[str]:
        if not path:
            return None
        return f"{self.IMAGE_BASE_URL}{path}"


tmdb_service = TMDBService(config.TMDB_API_KEY)
